}</style><script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

  const select = document.querySelector(
    'select.gmw-neurodivergency-field[data-form_id="66"]'
  );

  if (!select) return;

  const defaultValues = ['Focussed'];

  // 1. Preselect the value in the select
  defaultValues.forEach(value => {
    let option = Array.from(select.options).find(o => o.value === value);

    if (!option) {
      option = new Option(value, value, true, true);
      select.add(option);
    }

    option.selected = true;
  });

  // 2. Refresh Select2 UI
  jQuery(select).trigger('change');

  // 3. Sync helper tiles
  const helperPanelId = select.id.replace('gmw-', 'helpers-gmw-');
  const helperPanel = document.getElementById(helperPanelId);

  if (!helperPanel) return;

  helperPanel.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-tile').forEach(tile => {
    const value = tile.getAttribute('data-value');

    if (defaultValues.includes(value)) {
      tile.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true');
      tile.classList.add('is-selected');
    } else {
      tile.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false');
      tile.classList.remove('is-selected');
    }
  });

});

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

    // --- CONFIGURATION: CUSTOMIZE THIS ---
    const config = {
        containerId: 'directory-grid',
        // Define your quick filter buttons here
        quickFilters: ['All', 'Agencies','Community','Jobs', 'Training', 'Cleaning', 'Insurance','Support','Discussion','Providers', 'Sole Traders']
    };

    const gridContainer = document.getElementById(config.containerId);
    if (!gridContainer) return;

    const innerContainer = gridContainer.querySelector('.e-con-inner') || gridContainer;

    // --- 1. BUILD THE UI ---
    const root = document.createElement('div');
    root.id = 'directory-interface-root';

    // A. Chips Container
    const chipsContainer = document.createElement('div');
    chipsContainer.id = 'directory-chips';
    
    config.quickFilters.forEach(text => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.innerText = text;
        btn.className = 'dir-chip';
        if(text === 'All') btn.classList.add('active');
        
        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            // Update Active State
            document.querySelectorAll('.dir-chip').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
            btn.classList.add('active');
            
            // Set Search Text (Empty if All)
            const val = text === 'All' ? '' : text;
            searchInput.value = val;
            processSearch(val);
        });
        chipsContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });

    // B. Search Wrapper
    const searchWrapper = document.createElement('div');
    searchWrapper.id = 'directory-search-wrapper';

    const searchInput = document.createElement('input');
    searchInput.type = 'text';
    searchInput.id = 'directory-search-input';
    searchInput.placeholder = '🔍 Search...';

    const clearBtn = document.createElement('span');
    clearBtn.id = 'directory-search-clear';
    clearBtn.innerHTML = '✕';

    searchWrapper.appendChild(searchInput);
    searchWrapper.appendChild(clearBtn);

    // C. Counter
    const counter = document.createElement('div');
    counter.id = 'directory-counter';
    counter.innerText = ''; // Init empty

    // D. No Results Message
    const noResultsMsg = document.createElement('div');
    noResultsMsg.id = 'directory-no-results';
    noResultsMsg.innerHTML = '<h3>No matches found</h3><p>Try adjusting your search or filter.</p>';

    // Assemble Root
    root.appendChild(chipsContainer);
    root.appendChild(searchWrapper);
    root.appendChild(counter);

    // Inject Root before Grid
    if (innerContainer !== gridContainer && innerContainer.parentNode === gridContainer) {
         gridContainer.insertBefore(root, innerContainer);
    } else {
         gridContainer.insertBefore(root, gridContainer.firstChild);
    }
    
    // Inject No Results Message INSIDE grid
    innerContainer.appendChild(noResultsMsg);


    // --- 2. INDEX DATA ---
    let gridItems = [];
    const children = innerContainer.querySelectorAll('.e-child, .elementor-column');

    children.forEach(child => {
        const titleEl = child.querySelector('.elementor-image-box-title');
        const descEl  = child.querySelector('.elementor-image-box-description');
        const anchor  = child.querySelector('a');

        if (titleEl) {
            gridItems.push({
                element: child,
                titleRaw: titleEl.innerText, // Keep original for display
                descRaw: descEl ? descEl.innerText : '',
                title: titleEl.innerText.toLowerCase().trim(),
                description: descEl ? descEl.innerText.toLowerCase().trim() : '',
                anchor: anchor
            });
        }
    });


    // --- 3. LOGIC CORE ---
    function processSearch(termRaw) {
        const searchTerm = termRaw.toLowerCase().trim();
        let visibleCount = 0;

        gridItems.forEach(item => {
            const match = item.title.includes(searchTerm) || item.description.includes(searchTerm);

            if (match) {
                item.element.classList.remove('dir-hidden-item');
                visibleCount++;
            } else {
                item.element.classList.add('dir-hidden-item');
                item.element.style.order = ''; 
            }
        });

        // Sort Visible
        const visibleItems = gridItems.filter(i => !i.element.classList.contains('dir-hidden-item'));
        visibleItems.sort((a, b) => a.title.localeCompare(b.title));
        visibleItems.forEach((item, index) => item.element.style.order = index + 1);

        // UI Updates
        clearBtn.style.display = searchTerm.length > 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
        
        // Update Counter
        if (searchTerm === '') {
            counter.innerText = `Showing all ${gridItems.length} services`;
        } else {
            counter.innerText = `Found ${visibleCount} services`;
        }

        // Toggle No Results
        noResultsMsg.style.display = visibleCount === 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
        
        // Update URL (Optional - remove if annoying)
        const newUrl = new URL(window.location);
        if (searchTerm) {
            newUrl.searchParams.set('q', searchTerm);
        } else {
            newUrl.searchParams.delete('q');
        }
        window.history.replaceState({}, '', newUrl);
        
        // Sync Chips Visuals
        document.querySelectorAll('.dir-chip').forEach(btn => {
            const btnText = btn.innerText.toLowerCase();
            if (btnText === 'all') {
                 if (searchTerm === '') btn.classList.add('active');
                 else btn.classList.remove('active');
            } else {
                 if (searchTerm === btnText) btn.classList.add('active');
                 else btn.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });
    }


    // --- 4. EVENTS ---
    searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => processSearch(e.target.value));

    clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        searchInput.value = '';
        processSearch('');
        searchInput.focus();
    });

    // Make Cards Clickable
    gridItems.forEach(item => {
        if (item.anchor) {
            const card = item.element.querySelector('.elementor-widget-image-box') || item.element;
            card.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (window.getSelection().toString().length > 0) return;
                if (e.target.closest('a')) return;
                
                const url = item.anchor.getAttribute('href');
                const target = item.anchor.getAttribute('target');
                if (target === '_blank') window.open(url, '_blank');
                else window.location.href = url;
            });
        }
    });

    // --- 5. INIT FROM URL ---
    // If user refreshes page with ?q=jobs, restore that search
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const initialQuery = params.get('q');
    if (initialQuery) {
        searchInput.value = initialQuery;
        processSearch(initialQuery);
    } else {
        processSearch('');
    }

});

  const viewportWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;

  // Remove old labels if re run
  document.querySelectorAll('.overflow-debug-label').forEach(l => l.remove());

  document.querySelectorAll('*').forEach(el => {
    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scrollW = el.scrollWidth;

    if (scrollW > viewportWidth + 1) {
      const percent = ((scrollW / viewportWidth) * 100).toFixed(1);
      const styles = window.getComputedStyle(el);

      el.style.outline = '2px solid red';

      const label = document.createElement('div');
      label.className = 'overflow-debug-label';

      label.innerHTML = `
        <strong>Overflow</strong><br>
        ${Math.round(scrollW)}px (${percent}%)<br>
        width: ${styles.width}<br>
        max-width: ${styles.maxWidth}<br>
        min-width: ${styles.minWidth}<br>
        margin L/R: ${styles.marginLeft} / ${styles.marginRight}<br>
        padding L/R: ${styles.paddingLeft} / ${styles.paddingRight}<br>
        position: ${styles.position}
      `;

      label.style.cssText = `
        position: absolute;
        top: 0;
        left: 0;
        background: rgba(180,0,0,0.9);
        color: #fff;
        font-size: 11px;
        line-height: 1.3;
        padding: 4px 6px;
        z-index: 999999;
        pointer-events: none;
        max-width: 90vw;
        box-sizing: border-box;
      `;

      // Ensure element can contain absolute label
      if (styles.position === 'static') {
        el.style.position = 'relative';
      }

      el.appendChild(label);
    }
  });

  console.log('Overflow debug complete');
})();

</style><script>/* ===============================
   ICONS MODULE v1.0
   Adds inline SVG icons to GMW controls
   =============================== */
(function iconModule(){
  const form = document.querySelector('form.gmw-form');
  if (!form) return;

  /* 1) Inject a small SVG sprite once per page */
  function ensureSprite(){
    if (document.getElementById('gmw-icon-sprite')) return;
    const sprite = document.createElement('div');
    sprite.id = 'gmw-icon-sprite';
    sprite.style.position = 'absolute';
    sprite.style.width = '0';
    sprite.style.height = '0';
    sprite.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    sprite.innerHTML = `

  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
  
  
    
    
  
`;
    document.body.appendChild(sprite);
  }

  /* 2) Utility to create an SVG use element */
  function makeIcon(id, clazz){
    const svg = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'svg');
    svg.setAttribute('class', `gmw-icon ${clazz || ''}`.trim());
    svg.setAttribute('focusable', 'false');
    svg.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    svg.setAttribute('width', '1em');
    svg.setAttribute('height', '1em');
    svg.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 24 24');
    const use = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'use');
    use.setAttributeNS('http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink', 'href', `#$90814`);
    svg.appendChild(use);
    return svg;
  }

  /* 3) Inject minimal CSS so icons look crisp and labels collapse on small screens */
  function injectIconCSS(){
    if (document.getElementById('gmw-icons-css')) return;
    const css = document.createElement('style');
    css.id = 'gmw-icons-css';
    css.textContent = `
/* icon sizing and spacing */
.gmw-icon { display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: .45em; }
.gmw-btn-icon-only .gmw-icon { margin-right: 0; }

/* rotate helpers when expanded */
button[aria-expanded="true"] .gmw-rotate-chevron { transform: rotate(180deg); }
.gmw-rotate-chevron { transition: transform .18s ease; }

/* helper toggle buttons, hide text label on narrow screens */

  /* 4) Wire icons onto known controls */
  function decorateButtons(){
    // Per-field helper controls
    form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-controls').forEach(ctrl =&gt; {
      // Select All
      ctrl.querySelectorAll('.gmw-select-all').forEach(btn =&gt; {
        if (!btn.querySelector('.gmw-icon')) btn.prepend(makeIcon('gmw-check-all'));
      });
      // Clear All
      ctrl.querySelectorAll('.gmw-clear-all').forEach(btn =&gt; {
        if (!btn.querySelector('.gmw-icon')) btn.prepend(makeIcon('gmw-clear'));
      });
      // Show List toggle
      ctrl.querySelectorAll('.gmw-toggle-helpers').forEach(btn =&gt; {
        // make it icon first, text second for responsive hiding
        if (!btn.querySelector('.gmw-icon')) {
          const ico = makeIcon('gmw-chevron-down', 'gmw-rotate-chevron');
          btn.prepend(ico);
          // wrap existing text in span for easy hide on mobile
          const txt = document.createElement('span');
          txt.className = 'gmw-btn-text';
          txt.textContent = btn.textContent.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim() || 'Show List';
          btn.appendChild(txt);
          // remove duplicate original string before we appended the span
          btn.childNodes.forEach(n =&gt; {
            if (n.nodeType === 3) n.textContent = '';
          });
        }
      });
    });

    // Master bar, create a single toggle button with stateful icon
    const masterBar = form.querySelector('.gmw-helpers-master-bar');
    if (masterBar) {
      let btn = masterBar.querySelector('.gmw-master-toggle');
      if (!btn) {
        btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.type = 'button';
        btn.className = 'gmw-master-toggle';
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        btn.appendChild(makeIcon('gmw-expand', 'gmw-rotate-chevron'));
        const span = document.createElement('span');
        span.className = 'gmw-btn-text';
        span.textContent = 'Expand all';
        btn.appendChild(span);
        masterBar.innerHTML = ''; // replace any previous content
        const label = document.createElement('strong');
        label.textContent = 'Helper panels';
        masterBar.appendChild(label);
        masterBar.appendChild(btn);
      }
    }

    // Optional, add a pin icon next to Address label for a little polish
    const addrWrap = form.querySelector('.gmw-address-field-wrapper .gmw-field-label');
    if (addrWrap &amp;&amp; !addrWrap.querySelector('.gmw-icon')) {
      addrWrap.prepend(makeIcon('gmw-pin'));
    }

    // Optional, add a filter icon next to “Show Extra Filters” bar buttons if you use that pattern
    form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-more-filters-toggle button').forEach(b =&gt; {
      if (!b.querySelector('.gmw-icon')) b.prepend(makeIcon('gmw-filter'));
    });
  }

  decorateButtons();

  /* 5) Keep icons and button labels in sync with state */
  function syncStates(){
    // Per-field toggles, switch chevron direction via aria-expanded
    form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-toggle-helpers').forEach(btn =&gt; {
      const expanded = btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
      const use = btn.querySelector('use');
      const text = btn.querySelector('.gmw-btn-text');
      if (use) use.setAttributeNS('http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink', 'href', expanded ? '#gmw-collapse' : '#gmw-expand');
      if (text) text.textContent = expanded ? 'Hide List' : 'Show List';
    });

    // Master toggle reflects whether any helper panel is open
    const master = form.querySelector('.gmw-helpers-master-bar .gmw-master-toggle');
    if (master) {
      const helpers = Array.from(form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel'));
      const anyOpen = helpers.some(p =&gt; p.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false');
      master.setAttribute('aria-expanded', anyOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
      const use = master.querySelector('use');
      const txt = master.querySelector('.gmw-btn-text');
      if (use) use.setAttributeNS('http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink', 'href', anyOpen ? '#gmw-collapse' : '#gmw-expand');
      if (txt) txt.textContent = anyOpen ? 'Collapse all' : 'Expand all';
    }
  }

  // Initial sync
  syncStates();

  // 6) Event hooks, reuse your existing events where possible
  // Per-field toggle clicks, if your code already toggles aria-expanded and aria-hidden this just listens
  form.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const t = e.target.closest('.gmw-toggle-helpers');
    if (t) {
      // your existing handler flips aria-expanded, so queue a sync
      setTimeout(syncStates, 0);
    }
  });

  // Master bar click toggles all helper panels
  const master = form.querySelector('.gmw-helpers-master-bar .gmw-master-toggle');
  if (master) {
    master.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      const panels = Array.from(form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel'));
      const anyOpen = panels.some(p =&gt; p.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false');
      const willOpen = !anyOpen;
      panels.forEach(p =&gt; {
        const headerBtn = p.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.gmw-toggle-helpers');
        p.setAttribute('aria-hidden', willOpen ? 'false' : 'true');
        if (headerBtn) headerBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', willOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
      });
      syncStates();
    });
  }

  // Observe aria changes so icons stay accurate even if other code modifies states
  const mo = new MutationObserver(syncStates);
  mo.observe(form, { attributes: true, subtree: true, attributeFilter: ['aria-expanded', 'aria-hidden'] });

})();

  /* ========== 1) Inject CSS from JS ========== */
  const css = `

  function getRuleSetFor(select) {
    const id = (select.id || "").toLowerCase();
    const name = (select.name || "").toLowerCase();
    const labelText = ((select.closest(".gmw-form-field-wrapper")?.querySelector(".gmw-field-label")?.textContent) || "").toLowerCase();

    if (id.includes("languages") || name.includes("[30]") || labelText.includes("languages")) return LANGUAGE_RULES;
    return CATEGORY_RULES;
  }

  /* ========== 3) Grouping core ========== */
  function groupSelect(select) {
    // If already has optgroups, skip to avoid duplicating
    if (select.querySelector("optgroup")) return;

    const rules = getRuleSetFor(select);
    const options = Array.from(select.querySelectorAll("option"));

    // Keep current selection
    const selected = new Set(options.filter(o =&gt; o.selected).map(o =&gt; o.value));

    // Build buckets
    const buckets = new Map();
    rules.forEach(r =&gt; buckets.set(r.label, []));
    options.forEach(opt =&gt; {
      // ignore placeholder or empty value options
      if (!opt.value) return;
      const text = (opt.textContent || "").trim();
      const rule = rules.find(r =&gt; r.tests.some(re =&gt; re.test(text))) || rules[rules.length - 1];
      buckets.get(rule.label).push(opt);
    });

    // Rebuild DOM with optgroups in the rule order
    const frag = document.createDocumentFragment();
    buckets.forEach((list, label) =&gt; {
      if (!list.length) return;
      const og = document.createElement("optgroup");
      og.label = label;
      list.forEach(o =&gt; {
        const c = o.cloneNode(true);
        c.selected = selected.has(c.value);
        og.appendChild(c);
      });
      frag.appendChild(og);
    });

    // Replace options
    select.innerHTML = "";
    select.appendChild(frag);

    // Nudge Select2 to refresh, if present
    if (hasSelect2) {
      const $sel = jQuery(select);
      if ($sel.data("select2")) {
        // trigger a refresh without closing the dropdown
        $sel.trigger("change.select2");
      }
    }
  }

  // Apply to initial targets
  targets.forEach(groupSelect);

  // If Select2 initializes later, group again so dropdown shows headers
  if (hasSelect2) {
    setTimeout(() =&gt; targets.forEach(groupSelect), 250);
    setTimeout(() =&gt; targets.forEach(groupSelect), 800);
  }

  // Optional, watch for dynamically added selects marked with data-grouping="auto"
  const mo = new MutationObserver(() =&gt; {
    const newTargets = Array.from(form.querySelectorAll('select.gmw-multiselect-type-field[data-grouping="auto"]'))
      .filter(s =&gt; !s.querySelector("optgroup"));
    newTargets.forEach(groupSelect);
  });
  mo.observe(form, { childList: true, subtree: true });
});

/* ========== v2.5 + v2.7 helpers ========== */
function normText(s){ return String(s||"").toLowerCase().normalize("NFD").replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g,""); }

function getFieldKey(selectEl){
  // stable key for localStorage, prefers id then name then label text
  const id = selectEl.id || "";
  const nm = selectEl.name || "";
  const wrap = selectEl.closest(".gmw-form-field-wrapper, .gmw-xprofile-field-wrapper");
  const lbl = wrap &amp;&amp; wrap.querySelector(".gmw-field-label") ? wrap.querySelector(".gmw-field-label").textContent.trim() : "";
  return `gmw_faves::$90814`;
}

function loadFaves(selectEl){
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(getFieldKey(selectEl));
    return raw ? new Set(JSON.parse(raw)) : new Set();
  } catch(e){ return new Set(); }
}
function saveFaves(selectEl, set){
  try { localStorage.setItem(getFieldKey(selectEl), JSON.stringify(Array.from(set))); } catch(e){}
}

/* Build groups from :
   - uses 
   - or option.dataset.group
   - or auto A–Z buckets by first letter
*/
function buildGroupsFromSelect(selectEl){
  const groups = [];
  const byLabel = new Map();

  // First, try real 
  selectEl.querySelectorAll("optgroup").forEach(og=&gt;{
    const label = og.label || "Other";
    const items = Array.from(og.querySelectorAll("option")).map(o=&gt;({
      value:o.value, text:o.textContent.trim(), selected:o.selected
    }));
    if (items.length) {
      groups.push({ label, items });
      byLabel.set(label, items);
    }
  });

  if (groups.length) return groups;

  // Next, try data-group on 
  const opts = Array.from(selectEl.options).filter(o=&gt;o.value);
  const hasDataGroup = opts.some(o=&gt;o.dataset &amp;&amp; o.dataset.group);
  if (hasDataGroup) {
    const map = new Map();
    opts.forEach(o=&gt;{
      const g = (o.dataset.group || "Other").trim();
      if (!map.has(g)) map.set(g, []);
      map.get(g).push({ value:o.value, text:o.textContent.trim(), selected:o.selected });
    });
    return Array.from(map.entries()).map(([label,items])=&gt;({label,items}));
  }

  // Finally, A–Z buckets
  const az = new Map();
  opts.forEach(o=&gt;{
    const t = o.textContent.trim();
    const key = /^[A-Za-z]/.test(t) ? t[0].toUpperCase() : "#";
    if (!az.has(key)) az.set(key, []);
    az.get(key).push({ value:o.value, text:t, selected:o.selected });
  });
  return Array.from(az.entries()).sort((a,b)=&gt;a[0].localeCompare(b[0])).map(([label,items])=&gt;({label,items}));
}

	
/*----------------- Above added 8/9/2025 ----------------*/	
  function injectMasterHelpersBar() {
    const bar = document.createElement('div');
bar.className = 'gmw-helpers-master-bar';
bar.innerHTML = `
  <strong>Helper panels</strong>
  <button type="button" class="gmw-helpers-master-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
    <span class="triangle" aria-hidden="true">▼</span> Expand all
  </button>
`;
form.prepend(bar);
const masterBtn = bar.querySelector('.gmw-helpers-master-toggle');

masterBtn.addEventListener('click', () =&gt; {
  const helpers = form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel');
  const expanded = masterBtn.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';

  if (expanded) {
    // collapse all
    helpers.forEach(panel =&gt; {
      panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      const chev = panel.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.gmw-chevron');
      if (chev) chev.classList.remove('expanded');
    });
    masterBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    masterBtn.innerHTML = `<span class="triangle" aria-hidden="true">▼</span> Expand all`;
  } else {
    // expand all
    helpers.forEach(panel =&gt; {
      panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      const chev = panel.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.gmw-chevron');
      if (chev) chev.classList.add('expanded');
    });
    masterBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    masterBtn.innerHTML = `<span class="triangle" aria-hidden="true">▲</span> Collapse all`;
  }
});

    bar.addEventListener('click', e =&gt; {
      if (!(e.target instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
      const action = e.target.getAttribute('data-master');
      if (!action) return;
      const panels = form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel');
      panels.forEach(p =&gt; {
        const chevron = p.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.gmw-chevron');
        const isExpand = action === 'expand';
        p.setAttribute('aria-hidden', String(!isExpand));
        if (chevron) chevron.classList.toggle('expanded', isExpand);
      });
    });
  }

  function setupFieldHelpers(selectEl) {
    const wrapper = selectEl.closest('.gmw-form-field-wrapper');
    if (!wrapper) return;

    /* controls row */
	  //*************************************************************
// controls row
const controls = document.createElement('div');
controls.className = 'gmw-helper-controls';

const fieldId = selectEl.id || '';
const labelEl = wrapper.querySelector('label');
const fieldLabelText = labelEl ? labelEl.textContent.trim() : 'Options';

controls.innerHTML = `
  <button type="button" class="gmw-select-all">Select All</button>
  <button type="button" class="gmw-clear-all">Clear All</button>
  <button type="button" class="gmw-toggle-helpers" aria-controls="helpers-${fieldId}" aria-expanded="false">
    <span class="gmw-chevron" aria-hidden="true">▼</span>
    <span class="label">Show Helper</span>
  </button>
`;

// helper panel with grid of tiles, collapsed by default
const panel = document.createElement('div');
panel.className = 'gmw-helper-panel';
panel.id = `helpers-${fieldId}`;
panel.setAttribute('role', 'region');
panel.setAttribute('aria-label', fieldLabelText);
panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');

const grid = document.createElement('div');
grid.className = 'gmw-helper-grid';
grid.setAttribute('role', 'grid');
panel.appendChild(grid);

// insert, so the visual order is: label -&gt; select2 -&gt; controls -&gt; panel
selectEl.after(controls);
controls.after(panel);

// build tiles from options
const options = Array.from(selectEl.options)
  .filter(o =&gt; o.value)
  .sort((a, b) =&gt; a.text.localeCompare(b.text, 'en', { sensitivity: 'base' }));

options.forEach((opt, idx) =&gt; {
  const tile = document.createElement('button');
  tile.type = 'button';
  tile.className = 'gmw-helper-tile';
  tile.textContent = opt.textContent;
  tile.dataset.value = opt.value;
  tile.setAttribute('role', 'gridcell');
  tile.setAttribute('aria-selected', opt.selected ? 'true' : 'false');
  tile.tabIndex = idx === 0 ? 0 : -1;
  grid.appendChild(tile);
});

 controls.addEventListener('click', e =&gt; {
  const btn = e.target.closest('button');
  if (!btn) return;

  // Select All
  if (btn.classList.contains('gmw-select-all')) {
    Array.from(selectEl.options).forEach(o =&gt; { if (o.value) o.selected = true; });
    triggerChange(selectEl);
    syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid);

  // Clear All

    Array.from(selectEl.options).forEach(o =&gt; { if (o.value) o.selected = false; });
    triggerChange(selectEl);
    syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid);
    return;
  }

  // Toggle helper panel

    const expanded = btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
    const nextExpanded = !expanded;

    // reflect state on button
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(nextExpanded));

    // reflect state on panel
    panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', String(!nextExpanded));

    // update label and chevron
    const labelSpan = btn.querySelector('.label');
    const chevSpan  = btn.querySelector('.gmw-chevron');
    if (labelSpan) labelSpan.textContent = nextExpanded ? 'Hide Helper' : 'Show Helper';
    if (chevSpan)  chevSpan.textContent  = nextExpanded ? '▲' : '▼';
    return;
  }
});

// ****************************************************added 8/9/2025 above



// ****************************************************************

    /* clicking tiles toggles selection */
    grid.addEventListener('click', (e) =&gt; {
      const btn = e.target.closest('.gmw-helper-tile');
      if (!btn) return;
      const value = btn.getAttribute('data-value');
      toggleOption(selectEl, value);
      btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', isOptionSelected(selectEl, value) ? 'true' : 'false');
      triggerChange(selectEl);
    });

    /* keyboard navigation, arrows move focus, space or enter toggles */
    grid.addEventListener('keydown', (e) =&gt; {
      const tiles = Array.from(grid.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-tile'));
      const current = document.activeElement;
      const idx = tiles.indexOf(current);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      const cols = computeCols(grid, tiles);
      let nextIdx = idx;

      switch (e.key) {
        case 'ArrowRight': nextIdx = Math.min(idx + 1, tiles.length - 1); e.preventDefault(); break;
        case 'ArrowLeft':  nextIdx = Math.max(idx - 1, 0); e.preventDefault(); break;
        case 'ArrowDown':  nextIdx = Math.min(idx + cols, tiles.length - 1); e.preventDefault(); break;
        case 'ArrowUp':    nextIdx = Math.max(idx - cols, 0); e.preventDefault(); break;
        case ' ':
        case 'Enter':
          e.preventDefault();
          const value = current.getAttribute('data-value');
          toggleOption(selectEl, value);
          current.setAttribute('aria-selected', isOptionSelected(selectEl, value) ? 'true' : 'false');
          triggerChange(selectEl);
          return;
        default: return;
      }

      if (nextIdx !== idx) {
        tiles.forEach(t =&gt; t.tabIndex = -1);
        tiles[nextIdx].tabIndex = 0;
        tiles[nextIdx].focus();
      }
    });

    /* keep tiles in sync when user uses Select2 dropdown */
    if (hasSelect2) {
      jQuery(selectEl).on('change', () =&gt; syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid));
    } else {
      selectEl.addEventListener('change', () =&gt; syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid));
    }
  }

  function selectAll(selectEl, on) {
    Array.from(selectEl.options).forEach(opt =&gt; {
      if (opt.value) opt.selected = !!on;
    });
    triggerChange(selectEl);
  }

  function toggleOption(selectEl, value) {
    const opt = Array.from(selectEl.options).find(o =&gt; o.value === value);
    if (!opt) return;
    opt.selected = !opt.selected;
  }

  function isOptionSelected(selectEl, value) {
    const opt = Array.from(selectEl.options).find(o =&gt; o.value === value);
    return !!(opt &amp;&amp; opt.selected);
  }

  function syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid) {
  const selected = new Set(Array.from(selectEl.selectedOptions).map(o =&gt; o.value));
  grid.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-tile').forEach(tile =&gt; {
    const isSel = selected.has(tile.dataset.value);
    tile.setAttribute('aria-selected', isSel ? 'true' : 'false');
    tile.classList.toggle('is-selected', isSel);
  });
}

function triggerChange(selectEl) {
  if (window.jQuery &amp;&amp; jQuery.fn &amp;&amp; typeof jQuery.fn.select2 === 'function' &amp;&amp; jQuery(selectEl).data('select2')) {
    jQuery(selectEl).trigger('change');
  } else {
    selectEl.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
  }
}

  function computeCols(grid, tiles) {
    if (tiles.length &lt; 2) return 1;
    const firstTop = tiles[0].getBoundingClientRect().top;
    for (let i = 1; i  firstTop + 1) return i;
    }
    return tiles.length;
  }

  /* Select2 matcher that is a bit more permissive */
  function selectiveMatcher(params, data) {
    if (!params.term || params.term.trim() === '') return data;
    if (!data || !data.text) return null;
    const q = params.term.toLowerCase();
    const t = data.text.toLowerCase();
    return t.includes(q) ? data : null;
  }

  /* -------------- show or hide extra filters -------------- */
/* ========== v2.5 + v2.7 renderer ========== */

/************added below 8/9/2025 *****************/
function renderTilesGrouped(selectEl, grid){
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  // header row for search and favourites-only toggle
  const tools = document.createElement("div");
  tools.className = "gmw-helper-tools";
  tools.innerHTML = `
    <label class="gmw-helper-searchwrap" aria-label="Filter options in this list">
      
    </label>
    <label class="gmw-helper-faves-only">
      
      <span>Show only favourites</span>
    </label>
    <span id="helper-search-hint" class="sr-only">Type to filter visible tiles, results update as you type</span>
  `;
  grid.appendChild(tools);

  const searchInput = tools.querySelector(".gmw-helper-search");
  const favesOnly   = tools.querySelector(".gmw-helper-faves-toggle");

  const favourites = loadFaves(selectEl); // Set of option values

  // Build data, also split out favourites as a pseudo group
  const rawGroups = buildGroupsFromSelect(selectEl).map(g =&gt; ({
    label: g.label,
    items: g.items.map(it =&gt; ({...it})) // shallow copy
  }));

  function splitFaves(groups){
    const favItems = [];
    const nonFavGroups = groups.map(g=&gt;{
      const keep = [];
      g.items.forEach(it =&gt; {
        if (favourites.has(it.value)) favItems.push(it);
        else keep.push(it);
      });
      return { label:g.label, items: keep };
    }).filter(g =&gt; g.items.length);
    favItems.sort((a,b)=&gt;a.text.localeCompare(b.text, "en"));
    const result = [];
    if (favItems.length) result.push({ label:"Favourites", items: favItems, isFaves:true });
    return result.concat(nonFavGroups);
  }

  let groups = splitFaves(rawGroups);

  // container for groups
  const container = document.createElement("div");
  container.className = "gmw-helper-groups";
  grid.appendChild(container);

  function makeGroupSection(group){
    const section = document.createElement("section");
    section.className = "gmw-helper-group";
    section.setAttribute("role","group");
    section.setAttribute("aria-label", group.label);

    const head = document.createElement("div");
    head.className = "gmw-helper-group-head";

    const total = group.items.length;
    const selectedCount = group.items.filter(it =&gt; it.selected).length;

    head.innerHTML = `
      <div class="gmw-group-meta">
        <button type="button" class="gmw-helper-group-toggle" aria-expanded="true" aria-label="Toggle ${group.label}">
          <span class="gmw-chevron" aria-hidden="true">▸</span>
          <span class="gmw-group-label">${group.label}</span>
        </button>
        <span class="gmw-group-count" aria-live="polite">${selectedCount} selected of ${total}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="gmw-group-actions">
        <button type="button" class="gmw-group-select">Select Group</button>
        <button type="button" class="gmw-group-clear">Clear Group</button>
      </div>
    `;

    const body = document.createElement("div");
    body.className = "gmw-helper-group-body";
    body.setAttribute("data-open","true");

    const inner = document.createElement("div");
    inner.className = "gmw-helper-group-grid";

    group.items.forEach(it=&gt;{
      const tile = document.createElement("button");
      tile.type = "button";
      tile.className = "gmw-helper-tile";
      tile.dataset.value = it.value;
      tile.setAttribute("role","option");
      tile.setAttribute("aria-selected", it.selected ? "true" : "false");

      // star for favourites
      const starred = favourites.has(it.value);
      tile.innerHTML = `
        <span class="gmw-tile-label">${it.text}</span>
        <button type="button" class="gmw-fave">
          <span class="star" aria-hidden="true">${starred ? "★":"☆"}</span>
        </button>
      `;
      inner.appendChild(tile);
    });

    body.appendChild(inner);
    section.appendChild(head);
    section.appendChild(body);

    // interactions
    const toggle = head.querySelector(".gmw-helper-group-toggle");
    const countEl = head.querySelector(".gmw-group-count");
    const selectBtn = head.querySelector(".gmw-group-select");
    const clearBtn  = head.querySelector(".gmw-group-clear");

    toggle.addEventListener("click", e=&gt;{
      e.preventDefault();
      const expanded = toggle.getAttribute("aria-expanded")==="true";
      toggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", String(!expanded));
      body.setAttribute("data-open", String(!expanded));
      const chev = toggle.querySelector(".gmw-chevron");
      chev &amp;&amp; chev.classList.toggle("expanded", !expanded);
    });

    function updateGroupCount(){
      const values = group.items.map(i=&gt;i.value);
      const selected = Array.from(selectEl.selectedOptions).map(o=&gt;o.value);
      const inGroupSelected = selected.filter(v=&gt;values.includes(v)).length;
      countEl.textContent = `${inGroupSelected} selected of ${group.items.length}`;
    }

    selectBtn.addEventListener("click", e=&gt;{
      e.preventDefault();
      const values = new Set(group.items.map(i=&gt;i.value));
      Array.from(selectEl.options).forEach(o=&gt;{ if(values.has(o.value)) o.selected = true; });
      triggerChange(selectEl);
      syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid);
      updateGroupCount();
    });
    clearBtn.addEventListener("click", e=&gt;{
      e.preventDefault();
      const values = new Set(group.items.map(i=&gt;i.value));
      Array.from(selectEl.options).forEach(o=&gt;{ if(values.has(o.value)) o.selected = false; });
      triggerChange(selectEl);
      syncTilesFromSelect(selectEl, grid);
      updateGroupCount();
    });

    // clicks inside tiles, either toggle selection or pin
    inner.addEventListener("click", e=&gt;{
      const favBtn = e.target.closest(".gmw-fave");
      const tile = e.target.closest(".gmw-helper-tile");
      if (!tile) return;
      const val = tile.dataset.value;

      if (favBtn) {
        // toggle favourite
        const isStar = favourites.has(val);
        if (isStar) favourites.delete(val); else favourites.add(val);
        saveFaves(selectEl, favourites);
        favBtn.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isStar ? "false" : "true");
        favBtn.querySelector(".star").textContent = isStar ? "☆" : "★";

        // rebuild groups to move item in or out of Favourites
        rebuildAll();
        return;
      }

      // toggle selection
      const opt = Array.from(selectEl.options).find(o=&gt;o.value===val);
      if (!opt) return;
      opt.selected = !opt.selected;
      tile.setAttribute("aria-selected", opt.selected ? "true":"false");
      triggerChange(selectEl);
      updateGroupCount();
    });

    // keep count fresh when selection changes externally
    const refresh = ()=&gt;updateGroupCount();
    if (window.jQuery &amp;&amp; jQuery.fn &amp;&amp; jQuery.fn.select2 &amp;&amp; jQuery(selectEl).data("select2")) {
      jQuery(selectEl).on("change", refresh);
    } else {
      selectEl.addEventListener("change", refresh);
    }

    return section;
  }

  function buildAndPaint(){
    container.innerHTML = "";
    groups.forEach(g =&gt; container.appendChild(makeGroupSection(g)));
    applyFieldFilter(searchInput.value.trim());
  }

  // filter within visible groups by the top search box
  function applyFieldFilter(term){
    const q = normText(term);
    container.querySelectorAll(".gmw-helper-group").forEach(section=&gt;{
      let visibleInGroup = 0;
      section.querySelectorAll(".gmw-helper-tile").forEach(tile=&gt;{
        const label = tile.querySelector(".gmw-tile-label").textContent;
        const match = !q || normText(label).includes(q);
        tile.style.display = match ? "" : "none";
        if (match) visibleInGroup++;
      });
      // hide group if nothing matches
      section.style.display = visibleInGroup ? "" : "none";
    });
  }

  function rebuildAll(){
    // rebuild groups to reflect any favourite changes
    groups = splitFaves(rawGroups);
    buildAndPaint();
  }

  // interactions for tools
  searchInput.addEventListener("input", ()=&gt;applyFieldFilter(searchInput.value.trim()));
  favesOnly.addEventListener("change", ()=&gt;{
    if (favesOnly.checked) {
      // hide all non favourites groups
      container.querySelectorAll(".gmw-helper-group").forEach(sec=&gt;{
        const isFav = sec.querySelector(".gmw-group-label") &amp;&amp; sec.querySelector(".gmw-group-label").textContent.trim()==="Favourites";
        sec.style.display = isFav ? "" : "none";
      });
    } else {
      // show all, then reapply current filter if any
      container.querySelectorAll(".gmw-helper-group").forEach(sec=&gt;{ sec.style.display = ""; });
      applyFieldFilter(searchInput.value.trim());
    }
  });

  // initial paint
  buildAndPaint();
}

/************added above 8/9/2025 *****************/
  /* -------------- show or hide extra filters -------------- */
function setupShowHideExtraFilters() {
  const servicesWrapper = form.querySelector('.gmw-services-provided-field-wrapper');
  if (!servicesWrapper) return;

  // Which wrappers must always stay visible
  const alwaysVisibleSet = new Set(ALWAYS_VISIBLE.map(sel =&gt; form.querySelector(sel)).filter(Boolean));

  // Collect collapsible field wrappers after Services Provided
  const collapsible = [];
  let cursor = servicesWrapper.nextElementSibling;
  const resetWrapper = form.querySelector('.gmw-reset-form-field-wrapper'); // stop before reset
  while (cursor &amp;&amp; cursor !== resetWrapper) {
    if (cursor.classList &amp;&amp; cursor.classList.contains('gmw-form-field-wrapper') &amp;&amp; !alwaysVisibleSet.has(cursor)) {
      collapsible.push(cursor);
    }
    cursor = cursor.nextElementSibling;
  }
  if (collapsible.length === 0) return;

  // Collapsible container, start collapsed
  const container = document.createElement('div');
  container.className = 'gmw-collapsible is-collapsed';
  container.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  container.style.overflow = 'hidden';
  container.style.maxHeight = '0px'; // ensure contracted by default

  // Move nodes into container
  collapsible.forEach(node =&gt; container.appendChild(node));

  // Toggle bar, insert directly after Services Provided
  const bar = document.createElement('div');
  bar.className = 'gmw-more-filters-toggle';
  bar.innerHTML = `
    <button type="button" data-more="show" aria-controls="gmw-extra-filters" aria-expanded="false">
      Show Extra Filters
    </button>
    <button type="button" data-more="hide" aria-controls="gmw-extra-filters" aria-expanded="true" style="display:none">
      Hide Extra Filters
    </button>
  `;

  // Give the container an id for aria-controls
  container.id = 'gmw-extra-filters';

  // Insert order: bar then container
  servicesWrapper.after(bar);
  bar.after(container);

  // Open and close helpers
  function openContainer() {
    container.classList.remove('is-collapsed');
    container.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    // measure natural height each time in case content changed
    container.style.maxHeight = container.scrollHeight + 'px';
    bar.querySelector('[data-more="show"]').style.display = 'none';
    const hideBtn = bar.querySelector('[data-more="hide"]');
    hideBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
    hideBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    bar.querySelector('[data-more="show"]').setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
  }
  function closeContainer() {
    container.classList.add('is-collapsed');
    container.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    container.style.maxHeight = '0px';
    bar.querySelector('[data-more="hide"]').style.display = 'none';
    const showBtn = bar.querySelector('[data-more="show"]');
    showBtn.style.display = 'inline-block';
    showBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    bar.querySelector('[data-more="hide"]').setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
  }

  // Click handling
  bar.addEventListener('click', e =&gt; {
    const btn = e.target.closest('button[data-more]');
    if (!btn) return;
    const mode = btn.getAttribute('data-more');
    if (mode === 'show') openContainer();
    if (mode === 'hide') closeContainer();
  });

  // Keep height accurate when open and the window resizes
  window.addEventListener('resize', () =&gt; {
    if (container.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false') {
      container.style.maxHeight = container.scrollHeight + 'px';
    }
  });
}

});
/* ===============================
   STICKY HELPER HEADERS v2.0
   Keeps controls visible while scrolling long helper lists
   Adds smooth open/close behavior with smart scroll-into-view
   =============================== */
(function stickyHelperHeaders(){
  const form = document.querySelector('form.gmw-form');
  if (!form) return;

  // Inject minimal CSS for sticky header
  ensureStickyCSS();

  // Build sticky mini header inside each helper panel
  form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel').forEach(setupStickyForPanel);

  // Rebuild if panels are added later
  const mo = new MutationObserver(muts =&gt; {
    let needs = false;
    muts.forEach(m =&gt; {
      if ([...m.addedNodes].some(n =&gt; n.nodeType === 1 &amp;&amp; n.classList?.contains('gmw-helper-panel'))) {
        needs = true;
      }
    });
    if (needs) {
      form.querySelectorAll('.gmw-helper-panel').forEach(setupStickyForPanel);
    }
  });
  mo.observe(form, { childList: true, subtree: true });

  // Hook into existing per-field toggle buttons to smooth scroll when opening
  form.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const btn = e.target.closest('.gmw-toggle-helpers');
    if (!btn) return;
    const panel = document.getElementById(btn.getAttribute('aria-controls'));
    if (!panel) return;

    // Wait for your existing handler to flip aria values
    setTimeout(() =&gt; {
      const isOpen = panel.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false';
      if (isOpen) smoothScrollPanelIntoView(panel, 12); // small visual gap
    }, 0);
  });

  // Also support master toggle smooth scroll to the first opened panel
  form.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const master = e.target.closest('.gmw-helpers-master-bar .gmw-master-toggle');
    if (!master) return;
    setTimeout(() =&gt; {
      const firstOpen = form.querySelector('.gmw-helper-panel[aria-hidden="false"]');
      if (firstOpen) smoothScrollPanelIntoView(firstOpen, 12);
    }, 0);
  });

  /* ---------- functions ---------- */

  function setupStickyForPanel(panel){
    if (panel.dataset.stickyReady === '1') return;
    panel.dataset.stickyReady = '1';

    panel.classList.add('gmw-helper-panel--enhanced');

    // Find sibling controls to mirror into sticky bar
    const controls = panel.previousElementSibling?.classList?.contains('gmw-helper-controls')
      ? panel.previousElementSibling
      : null;

    // Build sticky strip
    const sticky = document.createElement('div');
    sticky.className = 'gmw-helper-sticky';
    sticky.setAttribute('role', 'toolbar');

    // Title, grab label text from aria-label on panel
    const title = document.createElement('div');
    title.className = 'gmw-helper-sticky__title';
    title.textContent = panel.getAttribute('aria-label') || 'Options';
    sticky.appendChild(title);

    // Selected count live badge
    const badge = document.createElement('div');
    badge.className = 'gmw-helper-sticky__count';
    badge.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
    badge.textContent = '0 selected';
    sticky.appendChild(badge);

    // Collapse button, mirrors per-field toggle
    const collapseBtn = document.createElement('button');
    collapseBtn.type = 'button';
    collapseBtn.className = 'gmw-helper-sticky__collapse';
    collapseBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Hide list');
    collapseBtn.appendChild(makeChevronIcon()); // uses icons module if present
    sticky.appendChild(collapseBtn);

    // Insert sticky at top of panel
    panel.prepend(sticky);

    // Events
    collapseBtn.addEventListener('click', () =&gt; {
      const toggle = panel.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('.gmw-toggle-helpers');
      if (!toggle) return;
      const expanded = toggle.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(!expanded));
      panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', String(expanded));
      // Sync icons module if present
      setTimeout(() =&gt; {
        const evt = new Event('gmw-helper-state-change', { bubbles: true });
        panel.dispatchEvent(evt);
      }, 0);
    });

    // Keep count in sync with select changes or tile changes
    const wrapper = panel.closest('.gmw-form-field-wrapper');
    const select = wrapper &amp;&amp; wrapper.querySelector('select.gmw-multiselect-type-field');
    const grid = panel.querySelector('.gmw-helper-grid');

    function updateCount(){
      let count = 0;
      if (select) count = Array.from(select.selectedOptions || []).length;
      badge.textContent = count === 0 ? '0 selected' : `${count} selected`;
    }
    updateCount();

    if (select) {
      select.addEventListener('change', updateCount);
      if (window.jQuery &amp;&amp; jQuery.fn &amp;&amp; jQuery.fn.select2) {
        jQuery(select).on('change', updateCount);
      }
    }
    if (grid) {
      grid.addEventListener('click', e =&gt; {
        if (e.target.closest('.gmw-helper-tile')) setTimeout(updateCount, 0);
      });
      grid.addEventListener('keydown', e =&gt; {
        if (e.key === ' ' || e.key === 'Enter') setTimeout(updateCount, 0);
      });
    }

    // ResizeObserver to keep sticky shadow active only when scrolled
    const scroller = panel;
    scroller.addEventListener('scroll', toggleShadow);
    const ro = new ResizeObserver(toggleShadow);
    ro.observe(scroller);

    function toggleShadow(){
      const atTop = scroller.scrollTop &lt;= 0;
      sticky.classList.toggle(&#039;is-shadowed&#039;, !atTop);
    }
  }

  function smoothScrollPanelIntoView(panel, gapPx){
    const rect = panel.getBoundingClientRect();
    const top = window.pageYOffset + rect.top - (gapPx || 0);
    window.scrollTo({ top, behavior: &#039;smooth&#039; });
  }
	//^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^ added 10/9/2026 %%%%%%%%%%%%%% below this line
function enforceHelperOrder(wrapper) {
  const select  = wrapper.querySelector(&#039;select.gmw-multiselect-type-field&#039;);
  const controls = wrapper.querySelector(&#039;.gmw-helper-controls&#039;);
  const panel    = wrapper.querySelector(&#039;.gmw-helper-panel&#039;);
  if (!select || !controls) return;

  // Prefer the rendered Select2 box if present
  const maybeS2 = select.nextElementSibling;
  const select2Container = (maybeS2 &amp;&amp; maybeS2.classList.contains(&#039;select2&#039;)) ? maybeS2 : select;

  // Only move if not already in the right place
  if (controls.previousElementSibling !== select2Container) {
   	 select2Container.after(controls);
  }
  if (panel &amp;&amp; controls.nextElementSibling !== panel) {
    controls.after(panel);
  }
}
	//^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^ added 10/9/2026 %%%%%%%%%%%%%% above this line
  function makeChevronIcon(){
    // Try to reuse the icon sprite from the icons module, fall back to text
    if (document.getElementById(&#039;gmw-icon-sprite&#039;)) {
      const svg = document.createElementNS(&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;, &#039;svg&#039;);
      svg.setAttribute(&#039;class&#039;, &#039;gmw-icon gmw-rotate-chevron&#039;);
      svg.setAttribute(&#039;width&#039;, &#039;1em&#039;);
      svg.setAttribute(&#039;height&#039;, &#039;1em&#039;);
      svg.setAttribute(&#039;viewBox&#039;, &#039;0 0 24 24&#039;);
      const use = document.createElementNS(&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;, &#039;use&#039;);
      use.setAttributeNS(&#039;http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink&#039;, &#039;href&#039;, &#039;#gmw-collapse&#039;);
      svg.appendChild(use);
      return svg;
    } else {
      const span = document.createElement(&#039;span&#039;);
      span.textContent = &#039;▲&#039;;
      return span;
    }
  }

  function ensureStickyCSS(){
    if (document.getElementById(&#039;gmw-sticky-helpers-css&#039;)) return;
    const css = document.createElement(&#039;style&#039;);
    css.id = &#039;gmw-sticky-helpers-css&#039;;
    css.textContent = `
/* Panel becomes local scroll container if content overflows */
.gmw-helper-panel.gmw-helper-panel--enhanced {
  position: relative;
  overflow: auto;
  max-height: clamp(240px, 50vh, 560px);
  border: 1px solid #A27D65;
  border-radius: 6px;
  background: #fff;
}

/* Sticky mini header inside panel */
.gmw-helper-sticky {
  position: sticky;
  top: 0;
  z-index: 1;
  display: flex;
  align-items: center;
  gap: 10px;
  padding: 8px 10px;
  background: linear-gradient(#fff, #fff);
  border-bottom: 1px solid #E9E1DC;
}

}</style><script>jQuery(function($) {
    let page = 2;
    let loading = false;
    const container = $('#user-articles-container');
    const loadMoreBtn = $('#mybp-loadmore');
    const loadingText = $('#mybp-loading em');

    function loadArticles() {
        if (loading) return;
        loading = true;
        loadingText.show();

        $.post(mybp_data.ajax_url, {
            action: 'mybp_load_more_articles',
            author_id: mybp_data.author_id,
            page: page
        }, function(data) {
            if (data.trim()) {
                container.append(data);
                page++;
                loading = false;
                loadingText.hide();
            } else {
                loadingText.text('No more articles.');
                loadMoreBtn.hide();
            }
        });
    }

    // Infinite scroll
    $(window).on('scroll', function() {
        if ($(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height() >= $(document).height() - 300) {
            loadArticles();
        }
    });

    // Fallback button
    loadMoreBtn.on('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        loadArticles();
    });
});

}</style><script>document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    var list = document.getElementById("serviceList");
    var items = list.getElementsByTagName("li");

    // Convert HTMLCollection to an array
    var itemsArr = Array.prototype.slice.call(items);

    // Sort the array alphabetically based on the label text
    itemsArr.sort(function(a, b) {
        var textA = a.querySelector(".gmw-checkbox-label").innerText;
        var textB = b.querySelector(".gmw-checkbox-label").innerText;
        return textA.localeCompare(textB);
    });

    // Append sorted items back to the list
    for (var i = 0; i < itemsArr.length; ++i) {
        list.appendChild(itemsArr[i]);
    }
});</script><style class="wpcode-css-snippet">.container {

					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];

					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
